+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor(INPUT0_SHAPE, S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor(WEIGHT_SHAPE, S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor(OUTPUT_SHAPE, S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_N
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // MFMA_TILE_K):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + MFMA_TILE_M
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * MFMA_TILE_K + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            k0 = kernel_offset // KERNEL_W
+            k1 = kernel_offset % KERNEL_W
+
+            if m0 < M_FLAT:
+                batch0 = m0 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial0 = m0 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // OUT_W
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % OUT_W
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < M_FLAT:
+                batch1 = m1 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial1 = m1 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // OUT_W
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % OUT_W
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + MFMA_TILE_M
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc11[acc_idx]
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,

+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

+            k0 = kernel_offset // KERNEL_W
+            k1 = kernel_offset % KERNEL_W

+

+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)

+        row10 = row00 + MFMA_TILE_M

+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_N
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // MFMA_TILE_K):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + MFMA_TILE_M
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * MFMA_TILE_K + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            k0 = kernel_offset // KERNEL_W
+            k1 = kernel_offset % KERNEL_W
+
+            if m0 < M_FLAT:
+                batch0 = m0 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial0 = m0 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // OUT_W
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % OUT_W
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < M_FLAT:
+                batch1 = m1 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial1 = m1 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // OUT_W
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % OUT_W
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + MFMA_TILE_M
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc11[acc_idx]

 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,
+        kernel_size: tuple,
+        stride: int = 1,
+        padding: int = 0,
+        dilation: int = 1,
+        groups: int = 1,
+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):
+        super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
+        self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(
+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._cached_weight = None
+        self._cached_weight_key = None
+
+    def _check_supported(self):
+        if self.conv2d.in_channels != IN_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports in_channels={IN_CHANNELS}.")
+        if self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports out_channels={OUT_CHANNELS}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports kernel_size={(KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.stride) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports stride=1.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.padding) != (0, 0):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports padding=0.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.dilation) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports dilation=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.groups != 1:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports groups=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.bias is not None:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel does not support bias.")

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_N
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // MFMA_TILE_K):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + MFMA_TILE_M
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * MFMA_TILE_K + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            k0 = kernel_offset // KERNEL_W
+            k1 = kernel_offset % KERNEL_W
+
+            if m0 < M_FLAT:
+                batch0 = m0 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial0 = m0 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // OUT_W
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % OUT_W
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < M_FLAT:
+                batch1 = m1 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial1 = m1 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // OUT_W
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % OUT_W
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + MFMA_TILE_M
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc11[acc_idx]
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,
+        kernel_size: tuple,
+        stride: int = 1,
+        padding: int = 0,
+        dilation: int = 1,
+        groups: int = 1,
+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):
+        super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
+        self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(
+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._cached_weight = None
+        self._cached_weight_key = None
+
+    def _check_supported(self):
+        if self.conv2d.in_channels != IN_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports in_channels={IN_CHANNELS}.")
+        if self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports out_channels={OUT_CHANNELS}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports kernel_size={(KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.stride) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports stride=1.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.padding) != (0, 0):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports padding=0.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.dilation) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports dilation=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.groups != 1:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports groups=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.bias is not None:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel does not support bias.")
 
-    def __init__(self, in_channels: int, out_channels: int, kernel_size: tuple, stride: int = 1, padding: int = 0, dilation: int = 1, groups: int = 1, bias: bool = False):
-            super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
-            self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size, stride=stride, padding=padding, dilation=dilation, groups=groups, bias=bias)
+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        self._check_supported()
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        key = (
+            x.device.type,
+            x.device.index,
+            x.dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cached_weight_key != key:
+            self._cached_weight = weight.detach().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_weight_key = key
+        return self._cached_weight

+
+BLOCK_M = 128
+BLOCK_N = 128
+WARP_TILE_M = 64
+WARP_TILE_N = 64
+MFMA_TILE_M = 32
+MFMA_TILE_N = 32
+MFMA_TILE_K = 8
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+
+N = 8
+IN_CHANNELS = 32
+IN_H = 512
+IN_W = 512
+OUT_CHANNELS = 64
+KERNEL_H = 5
+KERNEL_W = 9
+OUT_H = 508
+OUT_W = 504
+K_FLAT = IN_CHANNELS * KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W
+M_FLAT = N * OUT_H * OUT_W
+
+INPUT0_SHAPE = (N, IN_CHANNELS, IN_H, IN_W)
+OUTPUT_SHAPE = (N, OUT_CHANNELS, OUT_H, OUT_W)
+WEIGHT_SHAPE = (OUT_CHANNELS, IN_CHANNELS, KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)
+
+
+def _ceil_div(x: int, y: int) -> int:
+    return (x + y - 1) // y

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_N
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // MFMA_TILE_K):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + MFMA_TILE_M
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * MFMA_TILE_K + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            k0 = kernel_offset // KERNEL_W
+            k1 = kernel_offset % KERNEL_W
+
+            if m0 < M_FLAT:
+                batch0 = m0 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial0 = m0 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // OUT_W
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % OUT_W
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < M_FLAT:

+                spatial1 = m1 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // OUT_W
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % OUT_W
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < OUT_CHANNELS:

+
+            if n1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + MFMA_TILE_M
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]

 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
 
+
+BLOCK_M = 128
+BLOCK_N = 128
+WARP_TILE_M = 64
+WARP_TILE_N = 64
+MFMA_TILE_M = 32
+MFMA_TILE_N = 32
+MFMA_TILE_K = 8
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+
+N = 8
+IN_CHANNELS = 32
+IN_H = 512
+IN_W = 512
+OUT_CHANNELS = 64
+KERNEL_H = 5
+KERNEL_W = 9
+OUT_H = 508
+OUT_W = 504
+K_FLAT = IN_CHANNELS * KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W
+M_FLAT = N * OUT_H * OUT_W
+
+INPUT0_SHAPE = (N, IN_CHANNELS, IN_H, IN_W)
+OUTPUT_SHAPE = (N, OUT_CHANNELS, OUT_H, OUT_W)
+WEIGHT_SHAPE = (OUT_CHANNELS, IN_CHANNELS, KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_N
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // MFMA_TILE_K):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + MFMA_TILE_M
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * MFMA_TILE_K + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            k0 = kernel_offset // KERNEL_W
+            k1 = kernel_offset % KERNEL_W
+
+            if m0 < M_FLAT:
+                batch0 = m0 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial0 = m0 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // OUT_W
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % OUT_W
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < M_FLAT:
+                batch1 = m1 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial1 = m1 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // OUT_W
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % OUT_W
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + MFMA_TILE_M
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc11[acc_idx]
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels,
+        out_channels,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups=1,
+        bias=False,
+    ):
+        super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
+        self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(
+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._cached_weight = None
+        self._cached_weight_key = None
+
+    def _check_supported(self):
+        if self.conv2d.in_channels != IN_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports in_channels={IN_CHANNELS}.")
+        if self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports out_channels={OUT_CHANNELS}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports kernel_size={(KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.stride) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports stride=1.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.padding) != (0, 0):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports padding=0.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.dilation) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports dilation=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.groups != 1:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports groups=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.bias is not None:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel does not support bias.")
 
-    def __init__(self, in_channels: int, out_channels: int, kernel_size: tuple, stride: int = 1, padding: int = 0, dilation: int = 1, groups: int = 1, bias: bool = False):
-            super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
-            self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size, stride=stride, padding=padding, dilation=dilation, groups=groups, bias=bias)
+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x):
+        self._check_supported()
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        key = (
+            x.device.type,
+            x.device.index,
+            x.dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cached_weight_key != key:
+            self._cached_weight = weight.detach().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_weight_key = key
+        return self._cached_weight
 
     def forward(self, x):

+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")

 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels,
+        out_channels,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,

+        bias=False,

+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,

+    def _check_supported(self):

+        if self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports out_channels={OUT_CHANNELS}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_N
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // MFMA_TILE_K):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + MFMA_TILE_M
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * MFMA_TILE_K + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            k0 = kernel_offset // KERNEL_W
+            k1 = kernel_offset % KERNEL_W
+
+            if m0 < M_FLAT:
+                batch0 = m0 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial0 = m0 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // OUT_W
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % OUT_W
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < M_FLAT:
+                batch1 = m1 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial1 = m1 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // OUT_W
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % OUT_W
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + MFMA_TILE_M
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc11[acc_idx]

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_N
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // MFMA_TILE_K):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + MFMA_TILE_M
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * MFMA_TILE_K + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            k0 = kernel_offset // KERNEL_W
+            k1 = kernel_offset % KERNEL_W
+
+            if m0 < M_FLAT:
+                batch0 = m0 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial0 = m0 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // OUT_W
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % OUT_W
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < M_FLAT:
+                batch1 = m1 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial1 = m1 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // OUT_W
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % OUT_W
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + MFMA_TILE_M
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]

+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)

 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels,
+        out_channels,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups=1,
+        bias=False,
+    ):
+        super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
+        self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(
+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._cached_weight = None
+        self._cached_weight_key = None
+
+    def _check_supported(self):
+        if self.conv2d.in_channels != IN_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports in_channels={IN_CHANNELS}.")
+        if self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports out_channels={OUT_CHANNELS}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports kernel_size={(KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.stride) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports stride=1.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.padding) != (0, 0):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports padding=0.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.dilation) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports dilation=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.groups != 1:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports groups=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.bias is not None:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel does not support bias.")

def _collect_jit_dependencies(jit_fn) -> list:
    from substrate.runtime.jit import JITCallable

    seen = set()
    ordered = []

    def visit(current):
        finder = DependenciesFinder(current)
        finder.visit(current.parse())
        for dep in finder.dependencies:
            if dep in seen:
                continue
            seen.add(dep)
            visit(dep)
            ordered.append(dep)

    if not isinstance(jit_fn, JITCallable):
        return []

    visit(jit_fn)
    return ordered


def _build_import_module(jit_fns: list) -> ast.Module:
    import_nodes = []
    seen_imports = set()

    for fn in jit_fns:
        py_module = fn.parse()
        used_names = {node.id for node in ast.walk(py_module) if isinstance(node, ast.Name)}
        capture = fn.get_capture_scope()
        for name in sorted(used_names):
            value = capture.get(name)
            if isinstance(value, types.ModuleType):
                module_name = value.__name__
                key = (module_name, name if name != module_name else None)
                if key in seen_imports:
                    continue
                seen_imports.add(key)
                asname = None if name == module_name else name
                import_nodes.append(
                    ast.Import(names=[ast.alias(name=module_name, asname=asname)])
                )

    module = ast.Module(body=import_nodes, type_ignores=[])
    return ast.fix_missing_locations(module)


def compile_to_binary(src, target, opt_level: int = 2, options=None):
    constexprs_json = _serialize_constexprs(src)

    jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(src.fn)
    import_module = _build_import_module([src.fn, *jit_deps])

 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
 
+
+BLOCK_M = 128
+BLOCK_N = 128
+WARP_TILE_M = 64
+WARP_TILE_N = 64
+MFMA_TILE_M = 32
+MFMA_TILE_N = 32
+MFMA_TILE_K = 8
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+
+N = 8
+IN_CHANNELS = 32
+IN_H = 512
+IN_W = 512
+OUT_CHANNELS = 64
+KERNEL_H = 5
+KERNEL_W = 9
+OUT_H = 508
+OUT_W = 504
+K_FLAT = IN_CHANNELS * KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W
+M_FLAT = N * OUT_H * OUT_W
+
+INPUT0_SHAPE = (N, IN_CHANNELS, IN_H, IN_W)
+OUTPUT_SHAPE = (N, OUT_CHANNELS, OUT_H, OUT_W)
+WEIGHT_SHAPE = (OUT_CHANNELS, IN_CHANNELS, KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)
+
+
+def _ceil_div(x, y):
+    return (x + y - 1) // y

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_N
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // MFMA_TILE_K):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + MFMA_TILE_M
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * MFMA_TILE_K + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            k0 = kernel_offset // KERNEL_W
+            k1 = kernel_offset % KERNEL_W
+
+            if m0 < M_FLAT:
+                batch0 = m0 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial0 = m0 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // OUT_W
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % OUT_W
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < M_FLAT:
+                batch1 = m1 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial1 = m1 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // OUT_W
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % OUT_W
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + MFMA_TILE_M
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc11[acc_idx]
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels,
+        out_channels,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups=1,
+        bias=False,
+    ):
+        super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
+        self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(
+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._cached_weight = None
+        self._cached_weight_key = None
+
+    def _check_supported(self):
+        if self.conv2d.in_channels != IN_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports in_channels={IN_CHANNELS}.")
+        if self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports out_channels={OUT_CHANNELS}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports kernel_size={(KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.stride) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports stride=1.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.padding) != (0, 0):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports padding=0.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.dilation) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports dilation=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.groups != 1:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports groups=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.bias is not None:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel does not support bias.")
 
-    def __init__(self, in_channels: int, out_channels: int, kernel_size: tuple, stride: int = 1, padding: int = 0, dilation: int = 1, groups: int = 1, bias: bool = False):
-            super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
-            self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size, stride=stride, padding=padding, dilation=dilation, groups=groups, bias=bias)
+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x):
+        self._check_supported()
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        key = (
+            x.device.type,
+            x.device.index,
+            x.dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cached_weight_key != key:
+            self._cached_weight = weight.detach().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_weight_key = key
+        return self._cached_weight
 
     def forward(self, x):
-        if tuple(x.shape) != (8, 32, 512, 512) or x.dtype != torch.float32:
-            raise RuntimeError('This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.')

+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")
+        if not x.is_cuda:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel requires a CUDA/HIP device tensor.")

The dependency scan is clean for this module, so the remaining issue is inside MLIR generation for the kernel body itself. I’m reproducing `_generate_mlir` in a standalone script to get the direct current diagnostics without pytest’s accumulated stderr noise, then I’ll patch only the offending kernel constructs.

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_N
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // MFMA_TILE_K):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + MFMA_TILE_M
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * MFMA_TILE_K + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            k0 = kernel_offset // KERNEL_W
+            k1 = kernel_offset % KERNEL_W
+
+            if m0 < M_FLAT:
+                batch0 = m0 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial0 = m0 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // OUT_W
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % OUT_W
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < M_FLAT:
+                batch1 = m1 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial1 = m1 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // OUT_W
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % OUT_W
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < OUT_CHANNELS:

+
+            if n1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + MFMA_TILE_M
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_N
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // MFMA_TILE_K):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + MFMA_TILE_M
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * MFMA_TILE_K + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+            k0 = kernel_offset // KERNEL_W
+            k1 = kernel_offset % KERNEL_W
+
+            if m0 < M_FLAT:
+                batch0 = m0 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial0 = m0 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // OUT_W
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % OUT_W
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < M_FLAT:
+                batch1 = m1 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial1 = m1 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // OUT_W
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % OUT_W
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + MFMA_TILE_N
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + MFMA_TILE_M
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+
+        if row00 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row00 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row00 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col0 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < M_FLAT and col1 < OUT_CHANNELS:
+            batch = row10 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            spatial = row10 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+            out_h = spatial // OUT_W
+            out_w = spatial % OUT_W
+            Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc11[acc_idx]

 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels,
+        out_channels,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups=1,
+        bias=False,
+    ):

+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )

+        self._cached_weight_key = None
+
+    def _check_supported(self):
+        if self.conv2d.in_channels != IN_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports in_channels={IN_CHANNELS}.")
+        if self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports out_channels={OUT_CHANNELS}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports kernel_size={(KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.stride) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports stride=1.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.padding) != (0, 0):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports padding=0.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.dilation) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports dilation=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.groups != 1:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports groups=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.bias is not None:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel does not support bias.")

+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x):
+        self._check_supported()
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        key = (
+            x.device.type,
+            x.device.index,
+            x.dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+        )

+            self._cached_weight = weight.detach().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()

The direct repro pinned it down: this generator only accepts a much narrower expression subset inside kernels than the naive Python source suggests. I’m rewriting the kernel body to use literal constants and simpler control flow, especially removing global-shape symbols from arithmetic and splitting combined conditions, then I’ll rerun the standalone MLIR generation before pytest.

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(180):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + 32
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + 32
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // 45
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % 45
+            k0 = kernel_offset // 9
+            k1 = kernel_offset % 9
+
+            if m0 < 2048256:
+                batch0 = m0 // 256032
+                spatial0 = m0 % 256032
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // 504
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % 504
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < 2048256:
+                batch1 = m1 // 256032
+                spatial1 = m1 % 256032
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // 504
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % 504
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < 64:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < 64:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + 32
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + 32
+
+        if row00 < 2048256:
+            batch = row00 // 256032
+            spatial = row00 % 256032
+            out_h = spatial // 504
+            out_w = spatial % 504
+            if col0 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+            if col1 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < 2048256:
+            batch = row10 // 256032
+            spatial = row10 % 256032
+            out_h = spatial // 504
+            out_w = spatial % 504
+            if col0 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]
+            if col1 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc11[acc_idx]
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):

+    def _check_supported(self):
+        if self.conv2d.in_channels != IN_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports in_channels={IN_CHANNELS}.")
+        if self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports out_channels={OUT_CHANNELS}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports kernel_size={(KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.stride) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports stride=1.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.padding) != (0, 0):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports padding=0.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.dilation) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports dilation=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.groups != 1:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports groups=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.bias is not None:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel does not support bias.")
+
+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x):
+        self._check_supported()
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        key = (
+            x.device.type,
+            x.device.index,
+            x.dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cached_weight_key != key:
+            self._cached_weight = weight.detach().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_weight_key = key
+        return self._cached_weight

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(180):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + 32
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + 32
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // 45
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % 45
+            k0 = kernel_offset // 9
+            k1 = kernel_offset % 9
+
+            if m0 < 2048256:
+                batch0 = m0 // 256032
+                spatial0 = m0 % 256032
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // 504
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % 504
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < 2048256:
+                batch1 = m1 // 256032
+                spatial1 = m1 % 256032
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // 504
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % 504
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < 64:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < 64:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + 32
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + 32
+
+        if row00 < 2048256:
+            batch = row00 // 256032
+            spatial = row00 % 256032
+            out_h = spatial // 504
+            out_w = spatial % 504
+            if col0 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+            if col1 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < 2048256:
+            batch = row10 // 256032
+            spatial = row10 % 256032
+            out_h = spatial // 504
+            out_w = spatial % 504
+            if col0 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]
+            if col1 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc11[acc_idx]

+    def _check_supported(self):
+        if self.conv2d.in_channels != IN_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports in_channels={IN_CHANNELS}.")
+        if self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports out_channels={OUT_CHANNELS}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports kernel_size={(KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.stride) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports stride=1.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.padding) != (0, 0):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports padding=0.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.dilation) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports dilation=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.groups != 1:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports groups=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.bias is not None:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel does not support bias.")
+
+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x):
+        self._check_supported()
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        key = (
+            x.device.type,
+            x.device.index,
+            x.dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cached_weight_key != key:
+            self._cached_weight = weight.detach().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_weight_key = key
+        return self._cached_weight

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(180):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + 32
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + 32
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // 45
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % 45
+            k0 = kernel_offset // 9
+            k1 = kernel_offset % 9
+
+            if m0 < 2048256:
+                batch0 = m0 // 256032
+                spatial0 = m0 % 256032
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // 504
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % 504
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < 2048256:
+                batch1 = m1 // 256032
+                spatial1 = m1 % 256032
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // 504
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % 504
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < 64:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < 64:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + 32
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + 32
+
+        if row00 < 2048256:
+            batch = row00 // 256032
+            spatial = row00 % 256032
+            out_h = spatial // 504
+            out_w = spatial % 504
+            if col0 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+            if col1 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < 2048256:
+            batch = row10 // 256032
+            spatial = row10 % 256032
+            out_h = spatial // 504
+            out_w = spatial % 504
+            if col0 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]
+            if col1 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc11[acc_idx]
+
+

+    def _check_supported(self):
+        if self.conv2d.in_channels != IN_CHANNELS:

+        if self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports out_channels={OUT_CHANNELS}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):

+        if tuple(self.conv2d.stride) != (1, 1):

+        if tuple(self.conv2d.padding) != (0, 0):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports padding=0.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.dilation) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports dilation=1.")

+            self._cached_weight = weight.detach().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(180):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + 32
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + 32
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // 45
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % 45
+            k0 = kernel_offset // 9
+            k1 = kernel_offset % 9
+
+            if m0 < 2048256:
+                batch0 = m0 // 256032
+                spatial0 = m0 % 256032
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // 504
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % 504
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < 2048256:
+                batch1 = m1 // 256032
+                spatial1 = m1 % 256032
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // 504
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % 504
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < 64:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < 64:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + 32
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + 32
+
+        if row00 < 2048256:
+            batch = row00 // 256032
+            spatial = row00 % 256032
+            out_h = spatial // 504
+            out_w = spatial % 504
+            if col0 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+            if col1 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < 2048256:
+            batch = row10 // 256032
+            spatial = row10 % 256032
+            out_h = spatial // 504
+            out_w = spatial % 504
+            if col0 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]
+            if col1 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc11[acc_idx]

+    def _check_supported(self):
+        if self.conv2d.in_channels != IN_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports in_channels={IN_CHANNELS}.")
+        if self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports out_channels={OUT_CHANNELS}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports kernel_size={(KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.stride) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports stride=1.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.padding) != (0, 0):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports padding=0.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.dilation) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports dilation=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.groups != 1:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports groups=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.bias is not None:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel does not support bias.")
+
+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x):
+        self._check_supported()
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        key = (
+            x.device.type,
+            x.device.index,
+            x.dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cached_weight_key != key:
+            self._cached_weight = weight.detach().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_weight_key = key
+        return self._cached_weight

Implemented the MFMA-only conv kernel in [output_model_new.py](/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p62/optimization_rounds/round1/output_model_new.py), keeping the fixed `128 x 128` block tile, `2 x 2` warp grid, `32 x 32 x 8` BF16 MFMA fragments, and the required non-contiguous accumulator writeback mapping. The model path is cudagraph-safe on the weight side via `_get_cached_weight`, which reuses the device tensor until the weight storage pointer changes.

I also repointed the required callsites in [test_conv2d_asym.py](/workspace/substrate/test/examples/conv2d/amdgpu/test_conv2d_asym.py) and [bench_conv2d.py](/workspace/substrate/benchmark/conv2d/bench_conv2d.py), fixed the benchmark constructor to pass `(kernel_h, kernel_w)`, and wrote [case.txt](/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p62/optimization_rounds/round1/path/to/case.txt).

Validation: `python -m pytest /workspace/substrate/test/examples/conv2d/amdgpu/test_conv2d_asym.py` passed with `2 passed`.

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+
+    acc00 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc01 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc10 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    acc11 = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(180):
+        a_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag0 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag1 = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.bf16)
 
+        m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + lane_col
+        m1 = m0 + 32
+        n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+        n1 = n0 + 32
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_flat = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+            ic_local = k_flat // 45
+            kernel_offset = k_flat % 45
+            k0 = kernel_offset // 9
+            k1 = kernel_offset % 9
+
+            if m0 < 2048256:
+                batch0 = m0 // 256032
+                spatial0 = m0 % 256032
+                o0_0 = spatial0 // 504
+                o1_0 = spatial0 % 504
+                a_frag0[e] = S.convert(X[batch0, ic_local, o0_0 + k0, o1_0 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if m1 < 2048256:
+                batch1 = m1 // 256032
+                spatial1 = m1 % 256032
+                o0_1 = spatial1 // 504
+                o1_1 = spatial1 % 504
+                a_frag1[e] = S.convert(X[batch1, ic_local, o0_1 + k0, o1_1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n0 < 64:
+                b_frag0[e] = S.convert(W[n0, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            if n1 < 64:
+                b_frag1[e] = S.convert(W[n1, ic_local, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+        acc00 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag0, acc00)
+        acc01 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0, b_frag1, acc01)
+        acc10 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag0, acc10)
+        acc11 = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1, b_frag1, acc11)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        col0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+        col1 = col0 + 32
+        row00 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        row10 = row00 + 32
+
+        if row00 < 2048256:
+            batch = row00 // 256032
+            spatial = row00 % 256032
+            out_h = spatial // 504
+            out_w = spatial % 504
+            if col0 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc00[acc_idx]
+            if col1 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc01[acc_idx]
+
+        if row10 < 2048256:
+            batch = row10 // 256032
+            spatial = row10 % 256032
+            out_h = spatial // 504
+            out_w = spatial % 504
+            if col0 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col0, out_h, out_w] = acc10[acc_idx]
+            if col1 < 64:
+                Y[batch, col1, out_h, out_w] = acc11[acc_idx]
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels,
+        out_channels,
+        kernel_size,

+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,

+    def _check_supported(self):
+        if self.conv2d.in_channels != IN_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports in_channels={IN_CHANNELS}.")
+        if self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS:
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports out_channels={OUT_CHANNELS}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):
+            raise RuntimeError(f"This fused kernel only supports kernel_size={(KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)}.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.stride) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports stride=1.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.padding) != (0, 0):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports padding=0.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.dilation) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports dilation=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.groups != 1:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports groups=1.")
+        if self.conv2d.bias is not None:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel does not support bias.")
+
+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x):
+        self._check_supported()
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        key = (
+            x.device.type,
+            x.device.index,
+            x.dtype,
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+        )
+        if self._cached_weight_key != key:
+            self._cached_weight = weight.detach().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_weight_key = key
+        return self._cached_weight
